function cursor_on_search()
{
	document.Form.already_srch.value=document.Form.keyword.value;
		document.Form.keyword.value="";
		document.all.keyword.style.color="#262626";
}

function cursor_out_search()
{
	if(document.Form.keyword.value=="")
	{
		document.Form.keyword.value=document.Form.already_srch.value;
		document.all.keyword.style.color="#262626";
	}
}

<script type="text/javascript">
	var checkFirst = false;
	var lastKeyword = '';
	var loopSendKeyword = false;
	var key_value = -1;
	
	function startSuggest() {
		if (event.keyCode == 40) {
			max_cnt = document.Form.max_cnt.value;
			key_value = key_value +1;
			if (key_value == max_cnt) key_value = 0;
			for (ki = 0; ki < max_cnt; ki++) {
				on_target = eval("td_"+ki);
				if (ki == key_value) {
					on_target.style.backgroundColor = '#f5f5f5';
				}
				else {
					on_target.style.backgroundColor = '#ffffff';
				}
			}
			loopSendKeyword = false;
			if (key_value >= 0 && event.keyCode != 8) {
				if (key_value == 0) document.Form.keyword.value= document.divform.td_h_0.value;
				if (key_value == 1) document.Form.keyword.value= document.divform.td_h_1.value;
				if (key_value == 2) document.Form.keyword.value= document.divform.td_h_2.value;
				if (key_value == 3) document.Form.keyword.value= document.divform.td_h_3.value;
				if (key_value == 4) document.Form.keyword.value= document.divform.td_h_4.value;
				if (key_value == 5) document.Form.keyword.value= document.divform.td_h_5.value;
				if (key_value == 6) document.Form.keyword.value= document.divform.td_h_6.value;
				if (key_value == 7) document.Form.keyword.value= document.divform.td_h_7.value;
				if (key_value == 8) document.Form.keyword.value= document.divform.td_h_8.value;
				if (key_value == 9) document.Form.keyword.value= document.divform.td_h_9.value;
				if (key_value == 10) document.Form.keyword.value= document.divform.td_h_10.value;
				if (key_value == 11) document.Form.keyword.value= document.divform.td_h_11.value;
				if (key_value == 12) document.Form.keyword.value= document.divform.td_h_12.value;
				if (key_value == 13) document.Form.keyword.value= document.divform.td_h_13.value;
				if (key_value == 14) document.Form.keyword.value= document.divform.td_h_14.value;
			}			
		}
		else if (event.keyCode == 38) {
			max_cnt = document.Form.max_cnt.value;
			key_value = key_value -1;
			if (key_value <= -1) key_value = max_cnt-1;
			for (ki = 0; ki < max_cnt; ki++) {
				on_target = eval("td_"+ki);
				if (ki == key_value) {
					on_target.style.backgroundColor = '#f5f5f5';
				}
				else {
					on_target.style.backgroundColor = '#ffffff';
				}
			}
			loopSendKeyword = false;	
			if (key_value >= 0 && event.keyCode != 8) {
				if (key_value == 0) document.Form.keyword.value= document.divform.td_h_0.value;
				if (key_value == 1) document.Form.keyword.value= document.divform.td_h_1.value;
				if (key_value == 2) document.Form.keyword.value= document.divform.td_h_2.value;
				if (key_value == 3) document.Form.keyword.value= document.divform.td_h_3.value;
				if (key_value == 4) document.Form.keyword.value= document.divform.td_h_4.value;
				if (key_value == 5) document.Form.keyword.value= document.divform.td_h_5.value;
				if (key_value == 6) document.Form.keyword.value= document.divform.td_h_6.value;
				if (key_value == 7) document.Form.keyword.value= document.divform.td_h_7.value;
				if (key_value == 8) document.Form.keyword.value= document.divform.td_h_8.value;
				if (key_value == 9) document.Form.keyword.value= document.divform.td_h_9.value;
				if (key_value == 10) document.Form.keyword.value= document.divform.td_h_10.value;
				if (key_value == 11) document.Form.keyword.value= document.divform.td_h_11.value;
				if (key_value == 12) document.Form.keyword.value= document.divform.td_h_12.value;
				if (key_value == 13) document.Form.keyword.value= document.divform.td_h_13.value;
				if (key_value == 14) document.Form.keyword.value= document.divform.td_h_14.value;
			}
		}
		else {
			checkFirst = false;
			suggest_s();
		}
	}
	function suggest_s() {
		if (checkFirst == false) {
			setTimeout("sendKeyword();", 500);
			loopSendKeyword = true;
		}
		checkFirst = false;		
	}
	function sendKeyword() {
		if (loopSendKeyword == false) return;
		
		var keyword = document.Form.keyword.value;
		if (keyword == '') {
			lastKeyword = '';
			hide('suggest');
		} else if (keyword != lastKeyword) {
			lastKeyword = keyword;
			
			if (keyword != '') {
				var params = "keyword=" + keyword;
				sendRequest("../suggest/suggest_simple.php", params, displayResult, 'POST');
			} else {
				hide('suggest');
			}
		}
		setTimeout("sendKeyword();", 500);
	}
	function displayResult() {
		if (httpRequest.readyState == 4) {
			if (httpRequest.status == 200) {
				var resultText = httpRequest.responseText;
				
				var result = resultText.split('|');
				var count = parseInt(result[0]);
				document.Form.max_cnt.value = count;
				key_value = -1;
				var keywordList = null;
				if (count > 0) {
					keywordList = result[1].split(':+:');
					var html = '<table border=0 cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 width=100%><form name="divform"><tr><td bgcolor="#eeeeee" style="padding:5 15 5 15px;"><strong>추천 검색어</strong></td></tr>';
					for (var i = 0 ; i < keywordList.length ; i++) {
						var ky_str = keywordList[i];
						
						if (ky_str.length > 20) var ky_str = ky_str.substr(0,40)+"..";
						ky_str = ky_str.toUpperCase();
						//ky_str = ky_str.replace(document.Form.keyword.value.toLowerCase(), "<font color='#eb0c00' style='font-weight:bold;'>"+document.Form.keyword.value+"</font>");
						ky_str = ky_str.replace(document.Form.keyword.value.toUpperCase(), "<font color='#eb0c00' style='font-weight:bold;'>"+document.Form.keyword.value+"</font>");						
						
						html += "<tr height=25><td id='td_"+i+"' onmouseover=\"on_event('td_"+i+"', 'on');\" onmouseout=\"on_event('td_"+i+"', 'out')\" style='padding-left:8; padding-right:8px;'><a href=\"javascript:select2('"+
						        keywordList[i]+"')\"><font color='262626'>"+
						        ky_str+"</font></a><input type='hidden' name='td_h_"+i+"' value='"+keywordList[i]+"'></td></tr>";
					}
					html += '<tr height=1><td style="border-top:1px solid #dfdeda;"></td></tr><tr height="15"><td></td></tr>';
						html += '<tr><td style="padding:3 10 3 8px;"><table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" width="100%"><tr><td width="5">▶</td><td>&nbsp;<a href="http://www.schoolmusic.co.kr/lp_guarantee/index.php">최저가 110% 보상제~</a></td></tr></table></td></tr>';
	html += '<tr><td style="padding:3 10 3 8px;"><table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" width="100%"><tr><td width="5">▶</td><td>&nbsp;<a href="http://www.schoolmusic.co.kr/Shop/index.php3?var=Search&max_cnt=0&already_srch=%C3%D6%B0%ED%B4%D9+%C0%CC%BC%F8%BD%C5&keyword=%09+Schecter+CustomShop">쉑터 커스텀샵 입고!!!</a></td></tr></table></td></tr>';
	html += '<tr><td style="padding:3 10 3 8px;"><table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" width="100%"><tr><td width="5">▶</td><td>&nbsp;<a href="http://www.schoolmusic.co.kr/Shop/event.php?name=DropEffect">5브랜드 페달 가격파괴!! 최대 43% 할인</a></td></tr></table></td></tr>';
	html += '<tr><td style="padding:3 10 3 8px;"><table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" width="100%"><tr><td width="5">▶</td><td>&nbsp;<a href="http://www.schoolmusic.co.kr/Shop/index.php3?var=GoodList&large_number=1&middle_number=495">LTD 전세계 최저가</a></td></tr></table></td></tr>';
	html += '<tr><td style="padding:3 10 3 8px;"><table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" width="100%"><tr><td width="5">▶</td><td>&nbsp;<a href="http://www.schoolmusic.co.kr/Shop/index.php3?var=GoodList&large_number=1&middle_number=867">민트급전시 DEAN USA</a></td></tr></table></td></tr>';
					html += "<tr height=15><td></td></tr><tr height=25><td align='right' bgcolor='#eeeeee' onclick='javascript:hide(\"suggest\");' style='cursor:hand;'>닫기X&nbsp;&nbsp;</td></tr></form></table>";
					var listView = document.getElementById('suggestList');
					listView.innerHTML = html;
					
					show('suggest');
				} else {
					hide('suggest');
				}
			} else {
				//alert("에러 발생: "+httpRequest.status);
			}
		}
	}
	function on_event(td_name, flag) {
		var tmp = eval(td_name);
		if (flag == 'on') tmp.style.backgroundColor="#f5f5f5";
		if (flag == 'out') tmp.style.backgroundColor="#FFFFFF";
		
	}
	function select2(selectedKeyword) {
		document.Form.keyword.value = selectedKeyword;
		loopSendKeyword = false;
		checkFirst = false;
		hide('suggest');
		document.Form.submit();
	}
	function show(elementId) {
		var element = document.getElementById(elementId);
		if (element) {
			element.style.display = '';
		}
	}
	function hide(elementId) {
		var element = document.getElementById(elementId);
		if (element) {
			element.style.display = 'none';
		}
	}
	</script>

<script language="javascript">
var sitemapflag = 1;
function sitemap_open() {
	if (sitemapflag == 1) {
		document.getElementById("sitemap").style.visibility='';
		sitemapflag = 2;
	}
	else if (sitemapflag == 2) {
		document.getElementById("sitemap").style.visibility='hidden';
		sitemapflag = 1;
	}
}
function sitemap_close() {
	document.getElementById("sitemap").style.visibility='hidden';
	sitemapflag = 1;
}
function last_kw_fun_proc(val) {
	document.getElementById('keyword').value = val;
	document.Form.submit();
}
function searchkw_del(val, val2)  {
	cookie_del_frm.location.href="/MainPage/searchkw_del.php?kw="+val+"&mode=kw_del";
	document.getElementById(val2).style.display='none';
}
function kw_save_off() {
	if (confirm('기록된 검색어가 모두 삭제됩니다. 검색어저장 기능을 끄시겠습니까?')) {
		cookie_del_frm.location.href="/MainPage/searchkw_del.php?mode=off";
		//location.href="/MainPage/searchkw_del.php?mode=off";
		document.getElementById('search_gubun_area').innerHTML = '<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" width="100%"><tr><td width="10">&nbsp;</td><td bgcolor="#EEEEEE" style="padding:5px;" align="right" onClick="javascript:kw_save_on();">검색어저장켜기</td><td bgcolor="#EEEEEE" width="12">▲</td><td width="10">&nbsp;</td></tr></table>';
		document.getElementById('search_info_area').innerHTML = '검색어 저장 켜기를 클릭하면<br>검색어가 저장됩니다.';
		document.getElementById('search_info_area').style.height='100px';
	}
}
function kw_save_on() {
	cookie_del_frm.location.href="/MainPage/searchkw_del.php?mode=on";
	//location.href="/MainPage/searchkw_del.php?mode=on";
	document.getElementById('search_gubun_area').innerHTML = '<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" width="100%"><tr><td width="10">&nbsp;</td><td bgcolor="#EEEEEE" style="padding:5px; cursor:hand;" align="right" onClick="javascript:kw_save_off();">검색어저장끄기</td><td bgcolor="#EEEEEE" width="12">▼</td><td width="10">&nbsp;</td></tr></table>';
	document.getElementById('search_info_area').innerHTML = '최근 검색어가 없습니다.';
	document.getElementById('search_info_area').style.height='100px';
	document.getElementById('search_info_area').style.align='100px';
}
function srchform_chk(){
	var kw = document.Form.keyword.value.replace(/ /gi, '');
	
	if (kw == "") {
		alert('검색어를 입력하세요');
		return false;
	}
	else return true;
}

<script language="javascript">
window.onscroll = function () {
	var b=document.body.scrollTop;
	var cart_cnt = '0';

	if (cart_cnt == 1) b = b+30;
	if (cart_cnt == 2) b = b+80;
	if (cart_cnt >= 3) b = b+140;

	var tmp = "";
	var tmp_len = tmp.length - 1;
	tmp = tmp.substr(0, tmp_len);
	var tmp_arr = tmp.split("|");
	
	if (tmp != '') {
		for (i=1; i<=tmp_arr.length; i++) {
			if (tmp_arr[i] != '') {
				var tmp2 = eval("popimg_view_"+i);
				tmp2.style.top = b+420;
			}
		}
	}
}
</script>

<script language="javascript">
function submit_compare() {
	var f=document.forms['comparef']
	var chk=0;
	for(var i=0;i<f.length;i++) {
		if(f[i].name=='its[]') {
			if(f[i].checked) {
				chk++;
			}
		}
	}
	if(chk<2) {
		alert('비교할 상품을 2개 이상선택해주세요.');
	} else {
		f.submit();
	}
}
function chk_compare(f,chkf) {
	var chk=0;
	for(var i=0;i<f.length;i++) {
		if(f[i].name=='its[]') {
			if(f[i].checked) {
				chk++;
			}
		}
	}
	if(chk==0) {
		for(var i=0;i<f.length;i++) {
			if(f[i].name=='its[]') {
				f[i].disabled=false;
			}
		}
	} else if(chk>2) {
		for(var i=0;i<f.length;i++) {
			if(f[i].name=='its[]' && !f[i].checked) {
				f[i].disabled=true;
			}
		}
	} else {
		for(var i=0;i<f.length;i++) {
			if(f[i].name=='its[]') {
				if(f[i].getAttribute('LARGE_NO')==chkf.getAttribute('LARGE_NO')) {
	//				f[i].checked=true;
					f[i].disabled=false;
				} else {
					f[i].checked=false;
					f[i].disabled=true;
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
</script>

  <script language="javascript">
var getNowScroll = function(){ 
	var de = document.documentElement; 
	var b = document.body; 
	var now = {}; 
	
	now.X = document.all ? (!de.scrollLeft ? b.scrollLeft : de.scrollLeft) : (window.pageXOffset ? window.pageXOffset : window.scrollX); 
	now.Y = document.all ? (!de.scrollTop ? b.scrollTop : de.scrollTop) : (window.pageYOffset ? window.pageYOffset : window.scrollY); 
	
	return now; 
} 

var msgNowScroll = function(){ 
	nowScroll = getNowScroll(); 
	//alert(nowScroll.X + "," + nowScroll.Y); 
	if (nowScroll.Y >= 580) document.getElementById("all_Category_menu_area_container").style.display = 'block';
	else document.getElementById("all_Category_menu_area_container").style.display = 'none';
} 

setInterval(msgNowScroll, 100);
</script>

<script language="javascript">
function getCookieVal (offset) { 
	var endstr = document.cookie.indexOf (";", offset); 
	if (endstr == -1) endstr = document.cookie.length; 
	return unescape(document.cookie.substring(offset, endstr)); 
} 
function GetCookie (name) { 
	var arg = name + "="; 
	var alen = arg.length; 
	var clen = document.cookie.length; 
	var i = 0; 
	while (i < clen) { //while open 
		var j = i + alen; 
		if (document.cookie.substring(i, j) == arg) 
		return getCookieVal (j); 
		i = document.cookie.indexOf(" ", i) + 1; 
		if (i == 0) break; 
	} //while close 
	return null; 
} 
function SetCookie (name, value) { 
	var argv = SetCookie.arguments; 
	var argc = SetCookie.arguments.length; 
	var expires = (2 < argc) ? argv[2] : null; 
	var path = (3 < argc) ? argv[3] : null; 
	var domain = (4 < argc) ? argv[4] : null; 
	var secure = (5 < argc) ? argv[5] : false; 
	document.cookie = name + "=" + escape (value) + ((expires == null) ? "" : ("; expires=" + expires.toGMTString())) + ((path == null) ? "" : ("; path=" + path)) + ((domain == null) ? "" : ("; domain=" + domain)) + ((secure == true) ? "; secure" : ""); 
}
function layer_popup_close(val) {
	if(val == 1) document.getElementById("div_logic_pop").style.display = 'none';
}
function layer_popup_close_day(val) {
	if(val == 1) {
		document.getElementById("div_logic_pop").style.display = 'none';
		var ExpDate = new Date();
		ExpDate.setTime(ExpDate.getTime() + 1000*60*60*24); 
		SetCookie('div_pop_cookie', 'yes', ExpDate);
	}
}
//SetCookie('div_pop_cookie', '');
</script>

<div id='div_logic_pop' style="position:absolute; margin-left:50%; left:-551px;top:289px; width:0px; height:0px; z-index:999999;">
  <div style="postion:relative; left:50px; border:1px solid #888d95; background-color:FFF; width:370px; height:447px;">
    <table width="370" height="447" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">

function banner_roll() {
	var ban_arr = new Array();
	ban_arr[0] = new Array();
	ban_arr[1] = new Array();
	ban_arr[2] = new Array();
	ban_arr[3] = new Array();
	ban_arr[4] = new Array();
	ban_arr[5] = new Array();

	ban_arr[0]['img'] = 'http://img.schoolmusic.co.kr/shop_main_banner/glober_main_bannrer.jpg';
	ban_arr[0]['link'] = 'http://www.schoolmusic.co.kr/Shop/event.php?name=2015event/global26th/global26th';
	ban_arr[0]['alt'] = '스쿨뮤직 탑 글로벌 진입';		
	ban_arr[1]['img'] = 'http://img.schoolmusic.co.kr/shop_main_banner/Blackstar_test_event.jpg';
	ban_arr[1]['link'] = 'http://www.schoolmusic.co.kr/Shop/event.php?name=Blackstar_test_store';
	ban_arr[1]['alt'] = '사운드를 비교해 보세요!';		
	ban_arr[2]['img'] = 'http://img.schoolmusic.co.kr/shop_main_banner/bogner.jpg';
	ban_arr[2]['link'] = 'http://www.schoolmusic.co.kr/Shop/index.php3?var=GoodList&large_number=22&middle_number=2429';
	ban_arr[2]['alt'] = '보그너 페달 입고';		
	ban_arr[3]['img'] = 'http://img.schoolmusic.co.kr/shop_main_banner/Edwards_main2.jpg';
	ban_arr[3]['link'] = 'http://www.schoolmusic.co.kr/Shop/index.php3?var=GoodList&large_number=1&middle_number=2424';
	ban_arr[3]['alt'] = '에드워즈 입고';		
	ban_arr[4]['img'] = 'http://img.schoolmusic.co.kr/shop_main_banner/beyond.jpg';
	ban_arr[4]['link'] = 'http://www.schoolmusic.co.kr/Shop/index.php3?var=GoodList&large_number=1&middle_number=2430';
	ban_arr[4]['alt'] = '비욘드 기타 입고';		
	ban_arr[5]['img'] = 'http://img.schoolmusic.co.kr/shop_main_banner/ESP_USA.jpg';
	ban_arr[5]['link'] = 'http://www.schoolmusic.co.kr/Shop/index.php3?var=Search&max_cnt=&already_srch=Blackstar+ID%3ACore&keyword=USA%BB%E7%C0%BA%C7%B0';
	ban_arr[5]['alt'] = 'ESP USA 사은품';		
	
	
	var ban_cnt = '6';
	
	if (shop_banner_b_flag == ban_cnt) shop_banner_b_flag=0;
	
	document.getElementById('shop_banner_b_img').innerHTML = '<a href="'+ban_arr[shop_banner_b_flag]['link']+'"><img src="'+ban_arr[shop_banner_b_flag]['img']+'" alt="'+ban_arr[shop_banner_b_flag]['alt']+'" width="791" height="350" style="border:0px;"></a>';
	
	document.getElementById('shop_banner_text0').style.backgroundColor='#ffffff';
	document.getElementById('shop_banner_text1').style.backgroundColor='#ffffff';
	document.getElementById('shop_banner_text2').style.backgroundColor='#ffffff';
	document.getElementById('shop_banner_text3').style.backgroundColor='#ffffff';
	document.getElementById('shop_banner_text4').style.backgroundColor='#ffffff';
	document.getElementById('shop_banner_text5').style.backgroundColor='#ffffff';
	
	document.getElementById('shop_banner_text'+shop_banner_b_flag).style.backgroundColor='#dadada';
	
	shop_banner_b_flag = shop_banner_b_flag + 1;

}
setInterval(banner_roll, 5000);	
banner_roll();

function mouse_ove_img(img, url, num) {
	document.getElementById('shop_banner_b_img').innerHTML = "<a href='"+url+"'><img src='"+img+"' style='border:0px;'></a>";
	
	document.getElementById('shop_banner_text0').style.backgroundColor='#ffffff';
	document.getElementById('shop_banner_text1').style.backgroundColor='#ffffff';
	document.getElementById('shop_banner_text2').style.backgroundColor='#ffffff';
	document.getElementById('shop_banner_text3').style.backgroundColor='#ffffff';
	document.getElementById('shop_banner_text4').style.backgroundColor='#ffffff';
	document.getElementById('shop_banner_text5').style.backgroundColor='#ffffff';
	
	document.getElementById('shop_banner_text'+num).style.backgroundColor='#dadada';
	
	shop_banner_b_flag = num;
}
